<p>This article summarizes the events, album releases, and album release dates in <a href="/wiki/Hip_hop_music" title="Hip hop music">hip hop music</a> for the year 2012.</p>

<p></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Events">Events</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2012_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Events">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="January">January</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2012_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: January">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cory_Gunz" title="Cory Gunz">Cory Gunz</a> was arrested for possessing a loaded firearm.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Azealia_Banks" title="Azealia Banks">Azealia Banks</a> signs to <a href="/wiki/Universal_Music" title="Universal Music" class="mw-redirect">Universal Music</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1"><span>[</span>1<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="February">February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2012_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kanye_West" title="Kanye West">Kanye West</a> won four <a href="/wiki/Grammy_Award" title="Grammy Award">Grammy Awards</a> for Best Rap Song, Best Rap Album, Best Rap Performance, and Best Rap/Sung Collaboration, while <a href="/wiki/Jay-Z" title="Jay-Z">Jay-Z</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kid_Cudi" title="Kid Cudi">Kid Cudi</a> have won one each.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Philthy_Rich" title="Philthy Rich">Philthy Rich</a> and two more people are arrested for supposedly owning a stolen Bentley vehicle.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tyga" title="Tyga">Tyga</a>'s major label debut album, <i><a href="/wiki/Careless_World:_Rise_of_the_Last_King" title="Careless World: Rise of the Last King">Careless World: Rise of the Last King</a></i> was thought to be taken off the shelves due to an unauthorized usage of one of <a href="/wiki/Martin_Luther_King_Jr." title="Martin Luther King Jr." class="mw-redirect">Martin Luther King Jr.</a>'s speech. However, the issue is resolved and the released date would go as planned.</li>
<li>Bizarre has left <a href="/wiki/D12" title="D12">D12</a>, leaving the group with five members.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="March">March</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2012_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: March">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/T.I." title="T.I.">T.I.</a> announces he signed <a href="/wiki/Iggy_Azalea" title="Iggy Azalea">Iggy Azalea</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chipmunk_(rapper)" title="Chipmunk (rapper)" class="mw-redirect">Chip</a> and <a href="/wiki/Trae_Tha_Truth" title="Trae Tha Truth" class="mw-redirect">Trae Tha Truth</a> to <a href="/wiki/Grand_Hustle_Records" title="Grand Hustle Records">Grand Hustle Records</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Rap-Up_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rap-Up-2"><span>[</span>2<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3LittleDigs_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3LittleDigs-3"><span>[</span>3<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>An SUV that <a href="/wiki/Young_Buck" title="Young Buck">Young Buck</a> was a passenger in, was shot at 11 times, but the rapper was not injured.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/MTV" title="MTV">MTV</a> announces that <a href="/wiki/Top_Dawg_Entertainment" title="Top Dawg Entertainment">Top Dawg Entertainment</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles" title="Los Angeles">Los Angeles</a>-based <a href="/wiki/Independent_record_label" title="Independent record label">independent record label</a>, have closed a <a href="/wiki/Joint_venture" title="Joint venture">joint venture</a> <a href="/wiki/Recording_contract" title="Recording contract">deal</a> with <a href="/wiki/Interscope_Records" title="Interscope Records">Interscope Records</a> and <a href="/wiki/Aftermath_Entertainment" title="Aftermath Entertainment">Aftermath Entertainment</a>. Under the new deal, <a href="/wiki/Black_Hippy" title="Black Hippy">Black Hippy</a> member Kendrick Lamar's debut <a href="/wiki/Studio_album" title="Studio album" class="mw-redirect">studio album</a>, <i><a href="/wiki/Good_kid,_m.A.A.d_city" title="Good kid, m.A.A.d city" class="mw-redirect">good kid, m.A.A.d city</a></i> will be jointly released via Top Dawg/Interscope/<a href="/wiki/Aftermath_Entertainment" title="Aftermath Entertainment">Aftermath</a> while releases from the rest of Black Hippy (<a href="/wiki/Ab-Soul_(rapper)" title="Ab-Soul (rapper)" class="mw-redirect">Ab-Soul</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jay_Rock" title="Jay Rock">Jay Rock</a> and <a href="/wiki/Schoolboy_Q" title="Schoolboy Q">Schoolboy Q</a>) will be distributed via Top Dawg/Interscope.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4"><span>[</span>4<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tyga" title="Tyga">Tyga</a>'s tour bus was shot at several times in Omaha, Nebraska, but the rapper was not injured.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kon_Artis" title="Kon Artis" class="mw-redirect">Kon Artis</a> has left <a href="/wiki/D12" title="D12">D12</a>, leaving the group with 4 members.</li>
<li>March 9 marked the 15th Anniversary of the death of <a href="/wiki/The_Notorious_B.I.G." title="The Notorious B.I.G.">The Notorious B.I.G.</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bangladesh_(music_producer)" title="Bangladesh (music producer)" class="mw-redirect">Bangladesh</a> signs to <a href="/wiki/Cash_Money_Records" title="Cash Money Records">Cash Money Records</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5"><span>[</span>5<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="April">April</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2012_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: April">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Q-Tip_(musician)" title="Q-Tip (musician)">Q-Tip</a> has announced his signing to <a href="/wiki/Kanye_West" title="Kanye West">Kanye West</a>’s <a href="/wiki/G.O.O.D._Music" title="G.O.O.D. Music" class="mw-redirect">G.O.O.D. Music</a>/<a href="/wiki/Def_Jam" title="Def Jam" class="mw-redirect">Def Jam</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6"><span>[</span>6<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>At this year's <a href="/wiki/Coachella_Music_Festival" title="Coachella Music Festival" class="mw-redirect">Coachella Music Festival</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dr._Dre" title="Dr. Dre">Dr. Dre</a> and <a href="/wiki/Snoop_Dogg" title="Snoop Dogg">Snoop Dogg</a> surprised the audience with a performance from <a href="/wiki/2Pac" title="2Pac" class="mw-redirect">2Pac</a> via hologram image.</li>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/D12" title="D12">D12</a> member <a href="/wiki/Mr._Porter" title="Mr. Porter">Mr. Porter</a> announced his debut album.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="May">May</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2012_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: May">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Adam_Yauch" title="Adam Yauch">Adam Yauch</a> (known as MCA), one of the founding members of <a href="/wiki/Beastie_Boys" title="Beastie Boys">Beastie Boys</a>, died on May 4 aged 47.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7"><span>[</span>7<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Young_Buck" title="Young Buck">Young Buck</a> will be heading to prison for two months for gun possession.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2_Chainz" title="2 Chainz">2 Chainz</a> was arrested for possessing a set of brass knuckles.</li>
<li>In the song "Exodus 23:1", <a href="/wiki/Pusha_T" title="Pusha T">Pusha T</a> insulted <a href="/wiki/Cash_Money_Records" title="Cash Money Records">Cash Money Records</a>, igniting a beef between him and <a href="/wiki/Lil_Wayne" title="Lil Wayne">Lil Wayne</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lupe_Fiasco" title="Lupe Fiasco">Lupe Fiasco</a> and <a href="/wiki/Pete_Rock" title="Pete Rock">Pete Rock</a>’s beef over the former remaking the latter’s beat from “T.R.O.Y.” for “Around My Way (Freedom Ain’t Free).”</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Eminem" title="Eminem">Eminem</a> announced that he is working on his eighth studio album.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Shawn_Chrystopher" title="Shawn Chrystopher">Shawn Chrystopher</a> signs to Timbaland Productions.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8"><span>[</span>8<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="June">June</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2012_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: June">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nicki_Minaj" title="Nicki Minaj">Nicki Minaj</a> was pulled from performing at New York's Hot 97 Summer Jam because on-air DJ <a href="/wiki/Peter_Rosenberg" title="Peter Rosenberg">Peter Rosenberg</a> called her song "<a href="/wiki/Starships_(song)" title="Starships (song)">Starships</a>" bullshit, wack and corny.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lil_Phat" title="Lil Phat">Lil Phat</a> died on June 7 after he was shot multiple times in Atlanta.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/MTV" title="MTV">MTV</a> is reporting that on June 16, Chicago rapper <a href="/wiki/Chief_Keef" title="Chief Keef">Chief Keef</a> signed with <a href="/wiki/Interscope_Records" title="Interscope Records">Interscope Records</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9"><span>[</span>9<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>At W.i.P. nightclub the scuffle between <a href="/wiki/Chris_Brown_(American_entertainer)" title="Chris Brown (American entertainer)" class="mw-redirect">Chris Brown</a> and <a href="/wiki/Drake_(entertainer)" title="Drake (entertainer)" class="mw-redirect">Drake</a> continues to be under investigation, though both artists are saying they had nothing to do with the violent incident that left many bloodied and injured. Now Philly rapper <a href="/wiki/Meek_Mill" title="Meek Mill">Meek Mill</a>, who was also present during the late night fight, has come forward to back up their claims that they did not instigate the bottle-throwing brawl.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10"><span>[</span>10<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Funk_Volume" title="Funk Volume">Funk Volume</a> signs <a href="/wiki/Jarren_Benton" title="Jarren Benton">Jarren Benton</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11"><span>[</span>11<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="July">July</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2012_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: July">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>Member of <a href="/wiki/OFWGKTA" title="OFWGKTA" class="mw-redirect">OFWGKTA</a> <a href="/wiki/Frank_Ocean" title="Frank Ocean">Frank Ocean</a> published an <a href="/wiki/Open_letter" title="Open letter">open letter</a> on his <a href="/wiki/Tumblr" title="Tumblr">Tumblr</a> blog on July 4, recounting <a href="/wiki/Unrequited_love" title="Unrequited love">unrequited feelings</a> he had for a man when he was 19 years old, citing it as his first true love.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12"><span>[</span>12<span>]</span></a></sup> Members of the hip hop industry generally responded positively to the announcement.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13"><span>[</span>13<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Business_magnate" title="Business magnate">Business magnate</a> <a href="/wiki/Russell_Simmons" title="Russell Simmons">Russell Simmons</a> wrote a short congratulatory article in <i>Global Grind</i>, and support was voiced by <a href="/wiki/Beyonc%C3%A9" title="Beyoncé">Beyoncé</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jay-Z" title="Jay-Z">Jay-Z</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14"><span>[</span>14<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Tyler,_The_Creator" title="Tyler, The Creator">Tyler, The Creator</a> also tweeted his support for Ocean, along with other members of OFWGKTA.<sup id="cite_ref-NYDaily_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NYDaily-15"><span>[</span>15<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16"><span>[</span>16<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rockie_Fresh" title="Rockie Fresh">Rockie Fresh</a> signs to <a href="/wiki/Maybach_Music_Group" title="Maybach Music Group">Maybach Music Group</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17"><span>[</span>17<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="August">August</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2012_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: August">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>Philthy Rich is shot 3 times but is released from a hospital the day after the shooting.</li>
<li>Hip Hop executive Chris Lighty, founder of <a href="/wiki/Violator_(company)" title="Violator (company)">Violator</a> and who managed and worked with artists like <a href="/wiki/50_Cent" title="50 Cent">50 Cent</a> and <a href="/wiki/Busta_Rhymes" title="Busta Rhymes">Busta Rhymes</a>, was found dead due to possible suicide.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Freeway" title="Freeway" class="mw-redirect">Freeway</a> signs to <a href="/wiki/Babygrande_Records" title="Babygrande Records">Babygrande Records</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18"><span>[</span>18<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rittz" title="Rittz">Rittz</a> signs to <a href="/wiki/Strange_Music" title="Strange Music">Strange Music</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19"><span>[</span>19<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="September">September</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2012_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: September">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lil_Wayne" title="Lil Wayne">Lil Wayne</a> has officially passed Rock n Roll legend <a href="/wiki/Elvis_Presley" title="Elvis Presley">Elvis Presley</a> with the most appearances on the Billboard 100 with 109 (42 as a solo artist, 67 as a featured artist).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jay-Z" title="Jay-Z">Jay-Z</a> announced the opening of the <a href="/wiki/Barclays_Center" title="Barclays Center">Barclays Center</a> with a concert, including a hologram of <a href="/wiki/Notorious_B.I.G." title="Notorious B.I.G." class="mw-redirect">Notorious B.I.G.</a> and a new verse.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/50_Cent" title="50 Cent">50 Cent</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fat_Joe" title="Fat Joe">Fat Joe</a> have ended their feud, appearing on stage together at the 2012 BET Hip Hop Awards. Also on BET Hip Hop Awards, 50 Cent and his crew <a href="/wiki/G-Unit" title="G-Unit">G-Unit</a> have been involved into a fight with <a href="/wiki/Maybach_Music_Group" title="Maybach Music Group">Maybach Music Group</a>'s member <a href="/wiki/Gunplay_(rapper)" title="Gunplay (rapper)">Gunplay</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="October">October</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2012_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: October">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>After all problems at BET Hip Hop Awards, <a href="/wiki/50_Cent" title="50 Cent">50 Cent</a> started a beef with <a href="/wiki/French_Montana" title="French Montana">French Montana</a> after <a href="/wiki/Bad_Boy_Records" title="Bad Boy Records">Bad Boy</a>'s rapper commented negatively about 50 Cent's career. <a href="/wiki/G-Unit" title="G-Unit">G-Unit</a>'s boss responded on <a href="/wiki/Twitter" title="Twitter">Twitter</a> calling French Montana a "hoe".</li>
<li>50 Cent appeared in an video wearing <a href="/wiki/Gunplay_(rapper)" title="Gunplay (rapper)">Gunplay</a>'s chain of <a href="/wiki/Maybach_Music_Group" title="Maybach Music Group">Maybach Music Group</a> while bowling.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nelly" title="Nelly">Nelly</a> was detained in <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">Texas</a> after cops find heroin and 10 pounds of weed on his tour bus.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/P._Diddy" title="P. Diddy" class="mw-redirect">P. Diddy</a> suffered injuries to his neck, ribs, and collarbone, following a car accident on October 24.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lil_Wayne" title="Lil Wayne">Lil Wayne</a> suffered multiple seizures on a flight to Texas.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="December">December</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2012_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: December">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>Both <a href="/wiki/Young_Jeezy" title="Young Jeezy">Young Jeezy</a>'s label CTE (Corporate Thug Entertainement) and <a href="/wiki/Rick_Ross" title="Rick Ross">Rick Ross</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Maybach_Music_Group" title="Maybach Music Group">Maybach Music Group</a> merge with <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Records" title="Atlantic Records">Atlantic Records</a>.</li>
<li>Both <a href="/wiki/Jay-Z" title="Jay-Z">Jay-Z</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kanye_West" title="Kanye West">Kanye West</a> each have six Grammy nominations for the 2013 Grammy Awards, <a href="/wiki/Nas" title="Nas">Nas</a> has four, <a href="/wiki/Drake_(rapper)" title="Drake (rapper)">Drake</a> and <a href="/wiki/2_Chainz" title="2 Chainz">2 Chainz</a> each have three, <a href="/wiki/Andre_3000" title="Andre 3000" class="mw-redirect">Andre 3000</a>, <a href="/wiki/Big_Sean" title="Big Sean">Big Sean</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pusha_T" title="Pusha T">Pusha T</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lil_Wayne" title="Lil Wayne">Lil Wayne</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Wiz_Khalifa" title="Wiz Khalifa">Wiz Khalifa</a> each have two.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/The_Notorious_B.I.G." title="The Notorious B.I.G.">The Notorious B.I.G.</a> Autopsy was leaked by the Los Angeles Police Department and published by TMZ. The Los Angeles Police Department apologized for the leaked to Voletta Wallace and Biggie's Family.</li>
<li>On December 24, 2012, It was announced that Capital STEEZ, a close friend of <a href="/wiki/Joey_Badass" title="Joey Badass">Joey Badass</a> and member of Pro Era, died from a suspected suicide.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20"><span>[</span>20<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
